***sutler.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sutler.html>sutler</a> (53103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">soeteler</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zoetelaar</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sutler.html>sutler</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sutlers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who follows an army, selling provisions.</li></ol>

***swatch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a> (67226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language_in_northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:English language in northern England">Northern England</a> dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swache</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the counterfoil or counterstock of a tally</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1512); further etymology unknown. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">swach</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swath</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swathe</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">swæcc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">taste; flavour; odour; fragrance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">swatches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A piece, pattern, or sample, generally of cloth or a similar material.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></b> of the wallpaper up to see if the colors would match the room.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1821</b> June,  “Art. XVIII. The Ayrshire Legatees, or the Correspondence of the Pringle Family. From <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blackwood%27s_Magazine" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Blackwood | s Magazine">Blackwood's Magazine</a>”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Elihu_Hall" class="extiw" title="w:John Elihu Hall">John E[lihu] Hall</a>, editor, <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Port_Folio" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Port Folio">The Port Folio</a></cite>, volume XI, number 234, Philadelphia, <a href = vnd.unilang:pa.html>Pa</a>. |  Published by Harrison Hall, No. 5 North Eleventh street, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/8839957">8839957</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=rbQPAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA411">page 411</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[...] I beg you will go to Bailie Delap's shop, and get patterns of his <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> black bombaseen, and crape, and muslin, and bring them <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to the parsonage, the <a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a>'s morning. [...] You will get, likewise, <b>swatches</b> of mourning print, with the lowest prices.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b>,  Kristin Omdahl,  “Introduction”, in  <cite>Knitting outside the <a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>Swatch</a>: 40 Modern Motifs</cite>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F%2BW" class="extiw" title="w:F+W">Interweave</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=9gb4AgAAQBAJamp;pg=PA7">page 7</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I love knitting motif <b>swatches</b>. <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  Chloe <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>Swatch</a> Out!</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Spotlight, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_%26_Schuster" class="extiw" title="w:Simon amp; Schuster"><a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> amp; Schuster Children's Publishing Division</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=xvrvAwAAQBAJamp;pg=PA45">page 45</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Shall I give you some money now for the <b>swatches</b>?" asked <a href = vnd.unilang:mrs.html>Mrs</a>. Flynn. / "What's a <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></b></i>?" <a href = vnd.unilang:sophie.html>Sophie</a> asked suddenly. / "A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></b>," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Zoey, "<a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a little sample of fabric that people use to pick and choose what will work for them without having to buy a whole yard. And fabric <b>swatches</b> are free! So don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> worry."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A selection of such <a href = vnd.unilang:samples.html>samples</a> bound together.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A clump or portion of something.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b>,  Thomas Needham |  Ronald Pratt |  <a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>Helen</a> Tse |  <a href = vnd.unilang:deb.html>Deb</a> Watson |  <a href = vnd.unilang:nancy.html>Nancy</a> Wylie,  “Introduction”, in  <cite>The Art of Watercolor Painting: Master Techniques for Creating Stunning Works of Art in Watercolor</cite>, Irvine, Calif. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_T._Foster" class="extiw" title="w:Walter T. Compare the two <b>swatches</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:gustavo.html>Gustavo</a> S. <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A demonstration, an example, a proof.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1717</b>,  anonymous [William Wright],  <cite>The Comical History of the Marriage betwixt Fergusia and Heptarchus</cite>, Edinburgh |  Printed by Robert Brown, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/520532132">520532132</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=EUxgAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA15">page 15</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Pray <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a>, pay off the Old Debt, before I truſt you more New. <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1811</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Boston" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Boston">Thomas Boston</a>,  “Period XII”, in George Pritchard, editor, <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:memoirs.html>Memoirs</a> of the Life and Writings of the Reverend Thomas Boston, A.M. This I record once for all, for a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></b> of the hospitality of the parish; for <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> given this people a largeness of heart, to communicate of their substance, on these and other <a href = vnd.unilang:occasions.html>occasions</a> also.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tag or other small object attached to another item as a means of identifying its owner; a tally; <i>specifically</i> the counterfoil of a tally.
<ul><li><i>c.</i> <b>1512</b>, “The Booke of All the Directions and <a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>Orders</a> for Kepynge of My Lordes Hous Yerely. X. Intended to Illustrate and Preserve Several Valuable <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>Remains</a> of Old Times.</i> [...] <i>In Four <a href = vnd.unilang:volumes.html>Volumes</a></i>, volume IV, London: Printed for and published by Edward Jeffery, No. 11, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pall_Mall,_London" class="extiw" title="w:Pall Mall, London">Pall-Mall</a>, 1809, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/oclc/1867264">→OCLC</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=OoUcAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA73">page 73</a>:
<dl><dd>ITEM that the <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Clerkis of the Brevements entre all the Taillis of the Furniunturs in the Jornall Booke in the Countynghous every day furthwith after the <a href = vnd.unilang:brede.html>Brede</a> be delyveret to the Pantre and then the Stoke [<i>i.e.</i>, main part] of the Taill to by delyveret to the Baker and the <b>Swache</b> to the Pantler. [...] ITEM that the <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Clerkis of the Brevements entre all the Taills of the Brasyantors in the Jornall Booke in the Countynghous at every tyme furthwith after the Bere be delyveret into the Buttry and then the Stoke of the Taill to be delyveret to the Brewar and the <b>Swatche</b> to the <a href = vnd.unilang:butler.html>Butler</a>.</dd></dl></li>

Atkinson,  <cite>A Glossary of the Cleveland Dialect: Explanatory, Derivative, and Critical</cite>, London |  John Russell Smith, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soho_Square" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Soho Square">Soho Square</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/23927809">23927809</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=ecM1AQAAIAAJamp;pg=PA512">page 512</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>Swatch</a></b>, sb. [substantive] A wooden tally. / In the days of spinning-wheels and home-woven cloth, amp;c., it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> customary to <a href = vnd.unilang:affix.html>affix</a> <b>Swatches</b> to the various rolls of cloth sent to the dyer's, which in this part of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cleveland,_England" class="extiw" title="w:Cleveland, England">Cleveland</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> marked with the initials of the sender. <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the <i>Wh. Gl.</i> [<i>A Glossary of Yorkshire <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a> and Phrases Collected in Whitby and the Neighbourhood, by an Inhabitant</i> (London, 1855)] another mode of recognition <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> by cutting out a portion of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>Swatch</a></b>, and returning it to the bringer. This, when the dyeing <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> complete, on being fitted into the gap left, enabled the owner to recognise his own piece of cloth, or what not.</span>]</div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">swatches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">swatching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">swatched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To create a <a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a>, especially a sample of knitted fabric.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Swatching</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> important in knitting to obtain the correct gauge.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1976</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vogue_(magazine)" class="extiw" title="w:Vogue (magazine)">Vogue</a></cite>, volume 166, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cond%C3%A9_Nast" class="extiw" title="w:Condé Nast">Condé Nast Publications</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/0262-2130">0262-2130</a></small>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3331928">3331928</a></small>, page 482:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">This season, before you <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> think about the makeup you need, think about the <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a>/grey/<a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a>/brown colors—and the clothes—you've <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> seeing on the preceding pages (to remind you, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>'ve <b>swatched</b> some of them here).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:gail.html>Gail</a> Callahan,  “Show-off Patterns”, in  <cite>Hand Dyeing Yarn and Fleece: Dip-Dyeing, Hand-Painting, Tie-Dyeing, and Other Creative Techniques</cite>, North Adams, Mass. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Workman_Publishing_Company" class="extiw" title="w:Workman Publishing Company">Storey Publishing</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=KOEa1KFdFkACamp;pg=PA159">page 159</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>Swatching</b> may seem like a tedious chore when you're trying the gauge for a commercial yarn. But when you've just dyed your first skein of handpainted yarn, you'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be more than eager to see what it <a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a> like worked up into a pattern.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> Nelkin,  “Beaded Beauties”, in  <cite>Knockout Knits: New Tricks for Scarves, Hats, Jewelry, and Other Accessories</cite>, Potter Craft, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crown_Publishing_Group" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Crown Publishing Group">Crown Publishing Group</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=KMYJAwAAQBAJamp;pg=PA17">page 17</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">When I first learned how to knit, it didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> occur to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> that beads could be incorporated into knitting. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> I <b>swatched</b> and ripped, then <b>swatched</b> and ripped again—until I figured out how to get the beads to lie exactly where I <a href = vnd.unilang:wanted.html>wanted</a> them to be.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Origin unknown; originally used chiefly in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_of_England" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:East of England">East of England</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">swatches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A channel or passage of water between sandbanks, or between a sandbank and a seashore.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1801</b>,  John Ritchie,  “Instructions for Sailing in the Northern Part of the Bay of Bengal. Part I. Survey of the Coast from Point Palmiras to the Braces; of the Outlets of the <a href = vnd.unilang:ganges.html>Ganges</a>, and of the Interjacent Rivers from Hughly River to Roymongul”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Huddart" class="extiw" title="w:Joseph Huddart">[Joseph Huddart]</a>, editor, <cite>The Oriental Navigator; or, New Directions for Sailing to and from the East Indies, China, New Holland, amp;c. amp;c. amp;c. <span style="font-style: normal;">[...]</span></cite>, 2nd edition, London |  Printed and published by Robert Laurie and James Whittle, map, chart, amp; printsellers, No. 53, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fleet_Street" class="extiw" title="w:Fleet Street">Fleet-Street</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/859378040">859378040</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=FbwBAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA281">page 281</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It muſt be obſerved, that the paſſages, called <i>Cockerlees</i>, are no other than <b>ſwatches</b> through the Long-Sand.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1804</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a> Ritchie [<i>i.e.</i>, John Ritchie],  “Directions for Crossing the Head of the Bay of Bengal”, in William Herbert, William Nicholson, Samuel Dunn, and <a href = vnd.unilang:gabriel.html>Gabriel</a> Wright, <a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>, <cite>A New Nautical Directory for the East-India and China Navigation: <span style="font-style: normal;">[...]</span></cite>, 7th edition, London |  Printed by S. Couchman, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Throgmorton_Street" class="extiw" title="w:Throgmorton Street">Throgmorton-Street</a>, for and <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> by William <a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a>, No. 148, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leadenhall_Street" class="extiw" title="w:Leadenhall Street">Leadenhall-Street</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>Sold</a> by A. Arrowsmith, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rathbone_Place" class="extiw" title="w:Rathbone Place">Rathbone-Place</a>; and Blacks and Parry, Leadenhall-Street, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/36780343">36780343</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=65heAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA265">page 265</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>Swatch</a></b>, or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>Swatch</a></b> of no ground, a chaſm in the bank, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ſituated between the latitudes of 21° and 21° 22′ North, and the middle of it lies about 50 leagues Weſt of the meridian of the White Cliffs.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1853</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Lyell" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Lyell">Charles Lyell</a>,  “Deltas of the Mississippi, <a href = vnd.unilang:ganges.html>Ganges</a>, and Other Rivers Exposed to Tidal Action”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Principles_of_Geology" class="extiw" title="w:Principles of Geology">Principles of Geology; or, The Modern Changes of the Earth and Its Inhabitants Considered as Illustrative of Geology</a></cite>, new and entirely rev. edition, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D._Appleton_%26_Company" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:D. <p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sweet</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often as a term of address</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> much <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a>.</li>

***symbool.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:symbool.html>symbool</a> (3711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">symbole</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">symbolum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σύμβολον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súmbolon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Middle Dutch used the Latin form <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">symbolum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:symbool.html>symbool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:symbolen.html>symbolen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:symbooltje.html>symbooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A symbol, sign, character, glyph or anything of symbolic value</li>
<li>A (notably Chistian) creed</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***synagoge.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:synagoge.html>synagoge</a> (14895)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sinagoge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:synagoge.html>synagoge</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">synagōga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">συναγωγή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sunagōgḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">assembly, gathering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synagoge.html>synagoge</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synagogen.html>synagogen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synagoges.html>synagoges</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synagoge.html>synagogetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">syndicat</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***syntaxis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:syntaxis.html>syntaxis</a> (79156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:syntaxis.html>syntaxis</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σῠ́ντᾰξῐς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súntaxis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:syntaxis.html>syntaxis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>syntax <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">structure of language</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***synthetiseren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:synthetiseren.html>synthetiseren</a> (112472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">synthétiser</i> (from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">synthèse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">synthesis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>), cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">synthesize</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">synthetisieren</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:synthetiseren.html>synthetiseren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To synthesize, make a synthesis, summarise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (re)produce synthetically, e.g. using substitute ingredients</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:taai.html>taai</a> (5121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">taey</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tāi</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tāhi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tanhuz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zäh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tough</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taai.html>taai</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taaier.html>taaier</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">taaist</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tough, resilient</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> difficult to chew</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:taak.html>taak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">task</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:straf.html>straf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">punishment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
